0000587Wreathe[All Projects] Bugpublic2017-02-16 00:312017-07-06 00:40
ReporteradminAssigned Toadmin 
PrioritynormalSeverityminorReproducibilityhave not tried
Status assignedResolutionopen 
Product Version 
Target VersionFixed in Version 
Summary0000587: Crystallize: various improvements
Description* Have decrystallize verify checksums.
* Verify that the coal5 file can correctly be expanded to the original files before (or while?) uploading, and before deleting input files.
* Automate updating item access counts for fcache/localstorecache/scache: maybe ~once in every 10? 100? requests, divide the recorded access counts for each item by 2. That way, new requests will be weighted more heavily.
* Provide a tool to go through the stream registry, or optionally a specified folder of hashpointers, and back up each crystal used by it.
* Have sreg_fsck and other tools that use 'find' die immediately if any item fails
* Tool to fsck a directory of stream backups
* Refactor fcache and localstorecache (and possibly sreg_stream_read) to reduce code duplication (split out the bulk of the caching logic into its own library, or something)

Low priority:

* Provide a tool to get a .crystal pointer for a crystal that's already been uploaded
* Include information on the last time a stream was successfully read next to each stream pointer
* When reading from the crystal cache also use IA's files.xml data to verify that the retrieved data matches IA's stored checksum

Maybe:
* For single-stream sreg uploads, don't crystallize them but just compress/upload/encrypt the raw stream (make a new pointer type for this).
* Provide a tool to reset the item access counts for fcache/localstorecache/scache?
* Tool for sreg_copy_write-ing the current directory (or the item(s) specified on the command line) into the crystallize WorkDirectory and then sreging it back into place (to allow easy reading/editing)
* Tool to fsck the crystal cache (could possibly retrieve IA's files.xml checksums and fail if there's a mismatch, although that wouldn't apply to fcache in general due to it not being constrained to IA URLs)
* Move crystallize to a plugin system so instead of ia, things could be stored locally, or in other s3, etc.
* Include torrent file as an alternative checksum verification tool in and beside the crystal
TagsNo tags attached.

admin

2017-02-16 02:38

administrator   ~0000543

Last edited: 2017-03-03 15:11

View 8 revisions

 Done:
 * Have scache_copy_write copy the directory to copy to the WorkDirectory first, do the replacements there, and then move it into place. That way, if there isn't enough disk space in the destination for the unpacked data, it can still be copied.
 * 404 cf checksum: I'm not sure what it's the checksum *for*, but cf83e1357eefb8bdf1542850d66d8007d620e4050b5715dc83f4a921d36ce9ce47d0d13c5d85f2b0ff8318d2877eec2f63b931bd47417a81a538327af927da3e is the sha512 hash of what scache_read_stream returns when the new stream is not yet available.
 * separate pack directory
 * increase store retries
 * Include checksumming and retries for all stream reads (this will necessitate adding a checksum field to several pointer formats)
 * Cache unpacked LocalStore directories in the same manner as fcache
 * Rename scache to sreg (meaning stream registry instead of stream cache) since cache implies it can be safely deleted

Didn't do:
 * use switch statement for pointer types (no real need, since using elifs prevents the indentation increasing indefinitely, which is what I wanted to avoid by using switch)

BASH_FUNC_git-escape-path%%=() {  if [[ "$(wc -l <<< "$1")" == "1" ]] || [[ "$(wc -l <<< "$1")" == "0" ]]; then
 sed 's/./&\\/g' <<< "$1" | awk '{print "\\"$1}' | sed 's/.$//';
 else
 exit 1;
 fi
}
BASH_FUNC_rubberfs%%=() {  if [[ "$1" == "cd" ]]; then
 name="$2";
 if [ ! -n "$name" ]; then
 name="library";
 fi;
 cd "/Wreathe/.Resources/RubberFS/$name/mount" || exit 1;
 else
 "$(which rubberfs)" "$@";
 fi
}
BASH_FUNC_qlstash%%=() {  while [[ ! -z "$1" ]]; do
 echo "Items remaining to qlstash: ";
 echo "$@";
 fileToStash="$1";
 echo "Begun qlstashing $fileToStash.";
 ( targetFile="$(readlink -f "$1")";
 elen;
 cd "$(dirname "$targetFile")" || exit 1;
 rubberfs stash "$1";
 egup-exit );
 echo "Done qlstashing $fileToStash.";
 shift;
 done;
 printf "\033c";
 echo "Done qlstashing all items."
}
BASH_FUNC_git-absolute-path%%=() {  fullpath="$(readlink -f "$1")";
 gitroot="$(git rev-parse --show-toplevel)" || return 1;
 [[ $fullpath == *$(printf %q "$gitroot")* ]] && echo "${fullpath/$gitroot\//}"
}
BASH_FUNC_error-die%%=() {  source error-notify "$@"
}

BASH_FUNC_git-escape-path%%=() {  if [[ "$(wc -l <<< "$1")" == "1" ]] || [[ "$(wc -l <<< "$1")" == "0" ]]; then
 sed 's/./&\\/g' <<< "$1" | awk '{print "\\"$1}' | sed 's/.$//';
 else
 exit 1;
 fi
}
BASH_FUNC_rubberfs%%=() {  if [[ "$1" == "cd" ]]; then
 name="$2";
 if [ ! -n "$name" ]; then
 name="library";
 fi;
 cd "/Wreathe/.Resources/RubberFS/$name/mount" || exit 1;
 else
 "$(which rubberfs)" "$@";
 fi
}
BASH_FUNC_qlstash%%=() {  while [[ ! -z "$1" ]]; do
 echo "Items remaining to qlstash: ";
 echo "$@";
 fileToStash="$1";
 echo "Begun qlstashing $fileToStash.";
 ( targetFile="$(readlink -f "$1")";
 elen;
 cd "$(dirname "$targetFile")" || exit 1;
 rubberfs stash "$1";
 egup-exit );
 echo "Done qlstashing $fileToStash.";
 shift;
 done;
 printf "\033c";
 echo "Done qlstashing all items."
}
BASH_FUNC_git-absolute-path%%=() {  fullpath="$(readlink -f "$1")";
 gitroot="$(git rev-parse --show-toplevel)" || return 1;
 [[ $fullpath == *$(printf %q "$gitroot")* ]] && echo "${fullpath/$gitroot\//}"
}
BASH_FUNC_error-die%%=() {  source error-notify "$@"
}

BASH_FUNC_git-escape-path%%=() {  if [[ "$(wc -l <<< "$1")" == "1" ]] || [[ "$(wc -l <<< "$1")" == "0" ]]; then
 sed 's/./&\\/g' <<< "$1" | awk '{print "\\"$1}' | sed 's/.$//';
 else
 exit 1;
 fi
}
BASH_FUNC_rubberfs%%=() {  if [[ "$1" == "cd" ]]; then
 name="$2";
 if [ ! -n "$name" ]; then
 name="library";
 fi;
 cd "/Wreathe/.Resources/RubberFS/$name/mount" || exit 1;
 else
 "$(which rubberfs)" "$@";
 fi
}
BASH_FUNC_qlstash%%=() {  while [[ ! -z "$1" ]]; do
 echo "Items remaining to qlstash: ";
 echo "$@";
 fileToStash="$1";
 echo "Begun qlstashing $fileToStash.";
 ( targetFile="$(readlink -f "$1")";
 elen;
 cd "$(dirname "$targetFile")" || exit 1;
 rubberfs stash "$1";
 egup-exit );
 echo "Done qlstashing $fileToStash.";
 shift;
 done;
 printf "\033c";
 echo "Done qlstashing all items."
}
BASH_FUNC_git-absolute-path%%=() {  fullpath="$(readlink -f "$1")";
 gitroot="$(git rev-parse --show-toplevel)" || return 1;
 [[ $fullpath == *$(printf %q "$gitroot")* ]] && echo "${fullpath/$gitroot\//}"
}
BASH_FUNC_error-die%%=() {  source error-notify "$@"
}

BASH_FUNC_git-escape-path%%=() {  if [[ "$(wc -l <<< "$1")" == "1" ]] || [[ "$(wc -l <<< "$1")" == "0" ]]; then
 sed 's/./&\\/g' <<< "$1" | awk '{print "\\"$1}' | sed 's/.$//';
 else
 exit 1;
 fi
}
BASH_FUNC_rubberfs%%=() {  if [[ "$1" == "cd" ]]; then
 name="$2";
 if [ ! -n "$name" ]; then
 name="library";
 fi;
 cd "/Wreathe/.Resources/RubberFS/$name/mount" || exit 1;
 else
 "$(which rubberfs)" "$@";
 fi
}
BASH_FUNC_qlstash%%=() {  while [[ ! -z "$1" ]]; do
 echo "Items remaining to qlstash: ";
 echo "$@";
 fileToStash="$1";
 echo "Begun qlstashing $fileToStash.";
 ( targetFile="$(readlink -f "$1")";
 elen;
 cd "$(dirname "$targetFile")" || exit 1;
 rubberfs stash "$1";
 egup-exit );
 echo "Done qlstashing $fileToStash.";
 shift;
 done;
 printf "\033c";
 echo "Done qlstashing all items."
}
BASH_FUNC_git-absolute-path%%=() {  fullpath="$(readlink -f "$1")";
 gitroot="$(git rev-parse --show-toplevel)" || return 1;
 [[ $fullpath == *$(printf %q "$gitroot")* ]] && echo "${fullpath/$gitroot\//}"
}
BASH_FUNC_error-die%%=() {  source error-notify "$@"
}

BASH_FUNC_git-escape-path%%=() {  if [[ "$(wc -l <<< "$1")" == "1" ]] || [[ "$(wc -l <<< "$1")" == "0" ]]; then
 sed 's/./&\\/g' <<< "$1" | awk '{print "\\"$1}' | sed 's/.$//';
 else
 exit 1;
 fi
}
BASH_FUNC_rubberfs%%=() {  if [[ "$1" == "cd" ]]; then
 name="$2";
 if [ ! -n "$name" ]; then
 name="library";
 fi;
 cd "/Wreathe/.Resources/RubberFS/$name/mount" || exit 1;
 else
 "$(which rubberfs)" "$@";
 fi
}
BASH_FUNC_qlstash%%=() {  while [[ ! -z "$1" ]]; do
 echo "Items remaining to qlstash: ";
 echo "$@";
 fileToStash="$1";
 echo "Begun qlstashing $fileToStash.";
 ( targetFile="$(readlink -f "$1")";
 elen;
 cd "$(dirname "$targetFile")" || exit 1;
 rubberfs stash "$1";
 egup-exit );
 echo "Done qlstashing $fileToStash.";
 shift;
 done;
 printf "\033c";
 echo "Done qlstashing all items."
}
BASH_FUNC_git-absolute-path%%=() {  fullpath="$(readlink -f "$1")";
 gitroot="$(git rev-parse --show-toplevel)" || return 1;
 [[ $fullpath == *$(printf %q "$gitroot")* ]] && echo "${fullpath/$gitroot\//}"
}
BASH_FUNC_error-die%%=() {  source error-notify "$@"
}

2017-02-22 13:19

administrator   ~0000547

From https://github.com/jjjake/internetarchive/issues/183:

I've seen this a few times now, using internetarchive 1.4.0 in GNU/Linux with Python 2.7. The upload command is: ia upload "$CrystalID" --verify --retries=100 --metadata="subject:Uploaded using Crystallize $crystallizeVersion" --metadata="subject:1EA21BD8-DB7E-11E5-9733-728C37852114" --metadata=subject:"$crystalTitle" --metadata=subject:"$CrystalID" --metadata="collection:$crystalCollection" --delete "$CrystalTmpUploadFile"

Thanks!
